    <script>
     if (!document.phpAds_used)
        document.phpAds_used = ',';
    phpAds_random = new String(Math.random());
    phpAds_random = phpAds_random.substring(2, 11);

    var leadexpand = $('#leadexpand');
    $('#panoramabanner_wrapper').on('click', '.carousel', function() {
        var src = $(this).siblings('.carousel').removeClass('active').end()
                .addClass('active').data('src');
        leadexpand.attr('src', src.replace('{rand}', phpAds_random));
    });

    var banner_random = Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 1;
    $('#panoramabanner_wrapper .carousel:nth-child(' + banner_random + ')').click();
    </script>

        var bigboxCtrl = {
        getCurrent: function() {
            return parseInt($('#banner-bigbox-wrap .btn-slot-list button.active').data('slot'));
        },
        changeSlot: function(slot) {

            var _self = this;
            var context = $('#banner-bigbox-wrap');
            var slotBtn = context.find('.btn-slot-list button');
            var zoneName = $('.btn-slot-list').data('zone_name');
            slot = parseInt(slot);

            if (slot === _self.getCurrent())
                return false;

            slotBtn.removeClass('active');
            slotBtn.filter('[data-slot="' + slot + '"]').addClass('active');

           _dfpInline[zoneName]((( true ) ? '0' + slot : slot));
        },
        init: function() {
            var _self = this;
            $(document)
            .on('click', '#banner-bigbox-wrap .btn-slot-list button', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var el = $(this);
                _self.changeSlot(el.data('slot'));
            });
        }
    };
    bigboxCtrl.init();
    bigboxCtrl.changeSlot(Math.floor(Math.random() * 4) + 1);

    <section class="main-section section clearfloat" id="contentzone">
     <div class="contentheader">
      <a href="https://www.dogilike.com/content/" title="บทความน่าอ่าน">
       <p class="sectionweb">
        Dogilike
       </p>
       <h1 class="section_headtxt">
        บทความน่าอ่าน
        <img height="39" src="/2013/images/iconarticle.png" width="45"/>
       </h1>
      </a>
      <p class="section_desc">
       เรื่องน่ารู้เกี่ยวกับสุนัข เทคนิคการเลี้ยงและการดูแลสุขภาพน้องหมา ทิปส์การฝึกสุนัขเด็ดๆ
       <br/>
       และทุกเรื่องที่คนรักหมาต้องรู้ อัพเดททุกวัน

     <script>
      function actShowBookDetail(value, obj) {
                            var css = {
                                'position': 'absolute',
                                'z-index': '1',
                                'top': '52px',
                                'left': (value == 0) ? '82px' : '48px'
                            };
                            $('ul.book-box', obj).css(css).slideDown('slow', function () {
                                $(this).removeClass('hide');
                            });
                        }

                        $('a.attend').live('click', function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var thisObj = $(this);
                            var curActObj = thisObj.closest('.activityitem');
                            var prObj = thisObj.closest('.activityitem').find('.book-box');
                            thisObj.closest('.activityitem').addClass('current');
                            if ($(this).hasClass('clicked')) {
                                if (confirm('แน่ใจจิง ๆ นะ !!')) {
                                    $('ul.book-box').slideUp('slow', function () {
                                        $(this).addClass('hide');
                                    });
                                    var param = {mode: 'cancel', id: $('#a_id', prObj).val()};
                                    $.ajax({
                                        type: "POST",
                                        url: "/ajax/updateBookmark.php",
                                        data: param,
                                        dataType: 'json',
                                        success: function (res) {
                                            if (res.status == false) {
                                                alert(res.msg);
                                                return;
                                            } else {
                                                thisObj.removeClass('clicked');
                                                //$('.dil_lll, .tempword', curActObj).remove();
                                                curActObj.find('.textdetailbig').eq(0).html(res.contents);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            } else {
                                actShowBookDetail(Number($(this).attr('val')), curActObj);
                            }
                        });

                        $('ul.book-box a.submit').live('click', function (e) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            var prObj = $(this).closest('.book-box');
                            var curActObj = prObj.closest('.current');
                            var event_type = (Math.ceil(prObj.position().left) == 82) ? 0 : 1;
                            var mode = 'insert';
                            if ($('a.attend.clicked', curActObj).length > 0) {
                                mode = 'edit';
                            }
                            var param = {mode: mode, id: $('#a_id', prObj).val(), show: $('#startshow', prObj).val(), alerttime: $('#date_alert', prObj).val(), event_type: event_type};
                            $.ajax({
                                type: "POST",
                                url: "/ajax/updateBookmark.php",
                                data: param,
                                dataType: 'json',
                                success: function (res) {
                                    if (res.status == false) {
                                        alert(res.msg);
                                        return;
                                    } else {
                                        if (mode == 'insert') {
                                            $('a.attend[val=' + event_type + ']', curActObj).addClass('clicked');
                                        } else {
                                            $('a.attend', curActObj).toggleClass('clicked');
                                        }
                                        curActObj.find('.textdetailbig').first().html(res.contents);
                                        $('ul.book-box').slideUp('slow', function () {
                                            $(this).addClass('hide');
                                        });
                                    }
                                }
                            });
                        });

                        $('ul.book-box a.reset').live('click', function () {
                            $(this).parent().parent().slideUp('slow', function () {
                                $(this).removeClass('show').addClass('hide');
                                $('div.event').find('div.current').removeClass('current');
                            });
                        });

                        $('span.dil_lll .likeBub li.pp').live('click ', function (e) {
                            if ($('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list').length == 0) {
                                $('body').append('<div id="lightbox-d-checkin-today-list"></div>');
                            }
                            $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list').html($(this).parent().next().html());
                            $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list').lightbox_me({centered: true,
                                onLoad: function () {
                                    $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list div.box').css({'width': $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list div.box').width(), 'height': $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list div.box').height(), 'overflow': 'hidden'});
                                    $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list div.box').find('ul').addClass('scrollable');
                                    $('#lightbox-d-checkin-today-list div.box').modernScroll({scroll: 'y'});
                                }
                            });
                        });

                        $('.book-box .closedBB').live('click', function () {
                            var acitem = $(this).closest('.book-box');
                            $(this).closest('.book-box').slideUp('slow', function () {
                                //$(this).removeClass('show').addClass('hide');
                                acitem.removeClass('current');
                            });
                        });
     </script>
    </section>

				เค

          function getMobileOperatingSystem() {
	  var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor || window.opera;

		if (/android/i.test(userAgent)) {
			return "android";
		}

		if (/iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent) && !window.MSStream) {
			return "ios";
		}

		return "unknown";
